    //alert(document.cookie.slice(600));
	var header_class = '';
	if (!location.search.match(/\bdisplay=nojavascript/i))
		header_class += ' javascript';
	if (navigator.userAgent.match(/(Mobile|Android|WebOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|Blackberry|IEMobile|Opera Mini)/i))
		header_class += ' mobiledevice';
	if (navigator.userAgent.match(/(Chrome|Chromium)/i)) header_class += ' chrome-browser';
		else if (navigator.userAgent.match(/(Safari)/i)) header_class += ' safari-browser';	
		else if (navigator.userAgent.match(/(Firefox)/i)) header_class += ' firefox-browser';	
		else if (navigator.userAgent.match(/(Safari)/i)) header_class += ' safari-browser';	
		else if (navigator.userAgent.match(/(MSIE)/i)) header_class += ' explorer-browser';	
	if (location.search.match(/ViewOptions=[\w%,]*ItemViewHeadlines/i)) header_class += ' mode-headlines';
		else if (location.search.match(/ViewOptions=[\w%,]*ItemViewCovers/i)) header_class += ' mode-covers';	
		else if (document.cookie.match(/ViewOptions=[\w%,]*ItemViewHeadlines/i)) header_class += ' mode-headlines';
		else if (document.cookie.match(/ViewOptions=[\w%,]*ItemViewCovers/i)) header_class += ' mode-covers';
	if (000) alert(window.innerWidth + ' ~ ' + window.outerWidth + ' ~ ' + window.location + ' ~ ' + window.screen.width);
	if (000) alert(window.innerWidth+'/'+window.outerWidth+ ' | ' +window.innerHeight+'/'+window.outerHeight);
	if (location.search.match(/\bdisplay=(extract|email)\b/));
		else if (document.cookie.match(/UserVersionDesktop/i) || location.search.match(/\bdisplay=desktop/)) header_class += ' desktop';
		else if (document.cookie.match(/UserVersionTablet/i) || location.search.match(/\bdisplay=tablet/)) header_class += ' tablet';   
		else if (document.cookie.match(/UserVersionMobile/i) || location.search.match(/\bdisplay=tablet/)) header_class += ' mobile';  
		else if (window.innerWidth > 50 && window.innerWidth >= 1400 || window.outerWidth > 50 && window.outerWidth >= 1400) header_class += ' desktop';  
		else if (window.innerWidth > 50 && window.innerWidth <= 600 || window.outerWidth > 50 && window.outerWidth <= 600) header_class += ' mobile';  
		else if (window.innerWidth > 50 && window.innerWidth < 1080 || window.outerWidth > 50 && window.outerWidth <= 1080) header_class += ' tablet narrowscreen';  
		else header_class += ' desktop'; 
	if (!location.search.match(/\bdisplay=(extract|email)/))
